Your problem is that you are not connected to your mySQL database. Usual setting are `localhost` for the server - port 3306 - database name - username and password. Joomla does not create the database for you - that has to be done already at installtion - have you done that?

Fiona EllisTuesday, 1 February 2011 at 21:57 UTC

Hello there! Hmm I'm not sure what procedure your friend was asked to follow? I applied for my passport through IPS (Identity and Passport Services). Just followed the regular process (filled in the application I got from the post office, and mailed it in with all my supporting documents through the passport check and send service. Then I got my supporting documents back in the mail with a letter asking me to make an appointment with IPS for an interview (which just verifies that I really am the person my application stated I am to avoid identity theft). Then had my interview and my passport arrived in the mail one week later! Let me know if you have any other questions! :-)

15800869@facebook.comTuesday, 1 February 2011 at 21:57 UTC

Hello there! Hmm I'm not sure what procedure your friend was asked to follow? I applied for my passport through IPS (Identity and Passport Services). Then had my interview and my passport arrived in the mail one week later! Let me know if you have any other questions! :-)

Ben. I agree. I have been wrestling with this idea for ages, but while the book is autobiographical, there has to be an outer core of history also which then explores all the other points I raise. Everything else is woven around my life story and is only there to provide context. I have read your blog and the other day replied to an article but had to attend a meeting and could not further contribute. I was logged in under my blog name thulasizwe21 which I have registered but not started.lol. On June 16 last year on the 34th anniversary of the Soweto student uprising I had meant to launch an online newspaper but work and life got in the way. Thulasizwe is the name and it may yet see the light of day. Your work is very illuminating for those who have not thought all of our lives that we were special people. I have debates here with African Americans regarding the Black/White issue and the manner in which they have bought into the one drop rule. To see Halle Berry affirm that ignorant stance turned me apoplectic and I was paralyzed with anger for days afterwards. Still am. Are you from Mutare by any chance? I was born there, My father was Anthony Roberts. His mother was Angeline Pinto. My Mother who died when I was 4 years old was Joyce Lovejoy Jacobs. I know little about her so if you are from that neck of the woods, I would welcome any feedback from the elders back home. My brother is Haydon Roberts. I Look forward to collaborating on a project Benjamin. I have something in the works that I will unleash within the next two months that is sure to put the Mixed race question at the forefront of at least a few peoples' minds. Peace. Sinclair.

1607440588@facebook.comFriday, 5 November 2010 at 11:28 UTC

Hi Carl, I suspect I can never tell you when time will be right for you, that is something you have to recognise for yourself. I can only tell you what made me do it. I looked into the future, 5, 10 years from now and asked myself if I would like to be doing what I was doing at that time, because barring any unexpected changes, that is exactly what would happen. No. Next I asked myself whether I wanted to be in control of the changes that happen in my life or wait for example, to be made redundant/fired especially when the jobs/opportunities are drying up faster than a puddle in a desert. Again the answer was no. Forced change initiated by others is rarely positive change and you will never be ready for it. Finally, I scared the hell out of myself. I watched the pensioners getting on and off public transport on their way collect their miserly pensions and to the market to buy 2 sausages for tea and decided that that was not me. I am not about to allow myself to get there without trying to reach for something better. The chance for me to get out was the catalyst for change and I have used this as an excuse to change my life completely, even the wife is going. I am out to make me happy for a change. I know some of the guys at Synetrix see my leaving as pure madness, I, on the other hand, see being unhappy everyday as pure madness. Even Einstein said 'expecting the different results from doing the same thing is madness', exactly what will change if you don't make the change? Most people are scared to take a chance because they stand to lose everything they have got so far. Here is a thought, if you take a chance; you have the opportunity to gain so much more than what you have now - better car, better house, better wife, better finances but most of all, a period of fulfilment. On the other hand what is the worst that can happen in this country? You go on the dole. Can you live on the dole? Of course you can - hundreds of thousands of people do. Come to think of it, millions of people survive without the dole parachute all over the world. This is how far I am prepared to go. My wife returns with my two youngest children to Zimbabwe on the 29th December and she will be talking the vast majority of our savings - read pay-out. Her duty is to set up business (that is what she wants to do) and support those kids because I am going to take off and visit those countries in my project on the cheap and I have no idea when I will start making any reasonable amount of money from the project or from my writing/photographs/videos to be able to pay any sort of maintenance. My plans are the book will be published in the next 12 months even if I have to self-publish. Maybe I will have to stop with the tail between my legs and start again but so what? I have got this far once, why the hell can't I do it again? But you see that's me Carl. 9/10 times when I have a chance to choose between safe and happy 50% of the time, happiness is the one I choose. The fact that you took the time to write to me about the subject tells me that you are at the crossroads. Did Greg and my leaving act as a catalyst for Nick leaving? Not sure but he appears to be less stressed and happier now working for himself. Are we acting as the catalyst for you thinking about it? I bet we are but it is you that holds the ultimate decision. If you are not willing to lose anything, then you have to listen to them that say 'you have to live with it' and maybe try to be a music star when you retire at 67. On the other hand, do you want to be doing what you are doing now next year, the year after? No, then think about what it will take to give you, let's say 2 years, to try the other option. Can you live on £20K a year? Can you rent out your house and get a bedsit, with your saving could it sustain you for a while? What about selling the house, finding a 1 bed flat and have enough cash from the equity to 'pay yourself' enough to live and create with? If you are comfortable with the fact that it could all go to shit, then get the hell out. What both you and I have to be thankful about is that we are in the position to seriously consider the option. Many people especially in the 'rich' world pretend they are not in a position to consider going for broke but many are - it is only fear that stops them and they are the ones that end up buying 2 rashers of bacon at the market. If the shit hits the fan for me, I hope be sleeping next to some fit Latino broad in some favela in sunny Brazil 8-) Take care and let me know what you decide. Cheers Ben

718145425@facebook.comFriday, 5 November 2010 at 01:29 UTC

Hi Ben, Just wanted to get your advice just for a second. I haven’t really felt satisfied in IT for a couple of years, more so since Christmas when Crapita bought us. It’s almost a choice that no one in their right mind would consider doing. I feel a real need to leave more of my music in the world before I die, and I am just not able to put the effort into it because of my day job. I feel even more compelled to do this after my mum’s death, when I had the probably ‘obvious to everyone under these circumstances’ feeling that happiness is the most important thing, not money, or big cars etc. Also, it felt like the clock to the end had started ticking. What I want to ask you is this. I have some money in the bank, not a massive amount. I have loads of equity in my house, I have no kids, no dependents, no serious girlfriend etc And I am 43, so have some reasonable years left. At what point does ‘one’ know when it is time to make the change...? I have all the normal ‘am I good enough’, ‘can I survive’, ‘am I going to lose everything’ feelings, but, I am longing for that feeling of being alive again... I stay up late and am always tired, and as a result I begrudge my job because I blame it for not allowing me to realise my full potential with my music. I can’t figure out if I am being silly, or un realistic. As a result of all this, I simply don’t give a shit at work, and even though I am in some new fancy team that I have to meet with in London, I am practically making no effort, maybe in a sort of suicidal fashion. IE – If they sack me then I don’t have to make the big decision... Ben, how do we know when the time is right.....??

But for me to achieve this I will need sponsorship, to help with travel costs and equipment. Therefore I will be sending out sponsorship letters to various companies ASAP, hopefully they will see my vision. To help with any applications I'm asking if you could you send me some feedback via email, explaining what you enjoyed about my so far travel experiences to Jamaica and Thailand. You may need to refresh by looking at my FB page  What was your favourite moment/s  Did you feel part of the journey  Entertainment and quality of information.  More importantly do you think I could make a career out of travel vlogging if given the opportunity  Would you subscribe to my YouTube channel. I'm hoping on my next trip to have the correct photography and video equipment, which will add value and professionalism to my YouTube channel from the start. Having done some market research on YouTube, and watched loads of travel vlog videos I can see there is definitely a niche in the market for a 54 year old travel vlogger. Clinton Le GrangeFriday, 18 February 2011 at 07:55 UTC

Clinton Le Grange 17 February at 10:40 What is this group about and why you should invite your friends to join. i Goffal http://www.facebook.com/?sk=messages&tid=1811425495164#!/group.php?gid=30984049647 An upgrade for the Goffal mindset We inter-rupt your normal face book usage, of status updates, likes, groups, farmville, inboxing, and general chit chat, to old friends, close and distant, to bring you this urgent message from (V)ieome. Good Day Goffals I am glad that you are proud to shout loud that you are a Goffal. Allow me first to apologize for this interruption. I do, like many of you, appreciate the comforts of the everyday routine, the security of the familiar, the tranquility of repetition. I enjoy them as much as any bloke. But in the spirit of commemoration - whereby those important events of the past, usually associated with someone's death or the end of some awful bloody struggle, I thought we would take time to mark November the 1st as the annual i Goffal day, I will explain what an i Goffal is later in this chapter. "Words offer the means to meaning, and for those who will listen, the enunciation of truth." And the truth is there is something very wrong with the new generation of Zimbabwean goffal, isn't there? Yes, I understand, some of you's don't even like to be associated with the word goffal, you prefer coloured, mixed race, and some of you's, who live in Europe or USA, even accept, the if you not white you black banner. I am and will always be a goffal. At present our collective memory been infected with very disturbing trends, where once we had goffal teachers, doctors, engineers, nurses, cooks, brilliant house wifes, first class artisans etc, we now see the emergence of hustlers, ho's and pro's, suicide. Our elders have met to discuss the issue and seek solutions, but unfortunatly as is the case with most situations in life or our given human nature, we seek to tackle the symtoms not the cause. So what is the cause of this unfortunate evolution of the goffal mindset. P O V E R T Y ! Now I know it is common for many goffals to describe other goffals as lazy, or people who scandel, fight, rumour monger, but know to do that, is to paint us all with one brush. To say that the nature of the goffal is to pull others down, is to say that is your nature, and I know if you are reading this you are not like that. You have principals, morals, responsibilitys and our forefathers engraved within all of us the highest honour, that of respect, that we even greet people we are not related to as thus, "Hello Auntie, Hello Uncle, Howzit boota! " What is an i Goffal? Of late you may have noticed posters and t-shirts all proudly bearing the iGoffal Label, shouting loud and proud, you may have wondered, what is that about, who loudly calls themselves a dung beatles, kinda like a nigga calling himself nigga. The i Goffal is a brotherhood working together to evolve our collective memory. Working for change of mindset. I know right now, you have fear and doubt because of your own views of Goffals and you thinking it will never work, drops those doubt. Know who you are (temet nosce as plato would say). Embrace your black and white, arabian, what ever your heritage is. And I know while I embrace my black heritage, my great grand mother was and africa lady from Zvimba called Chiganan Shinawako, and I am very proud of that, the black Zimbabweans will never embrace me. In Zimbabwe we may have no place, no economic space and it is our duty as i Goffals to create that. I say to the elders, if you have a skill pass it on to the younger generation, give them that hope and pride that is need to reboot the goffal mindset. Dont be the master of your own demise by pulling your culture down, work to support and uplift each other. Let go of your pre-concieved notions that our culture or the people that in it are bad, because we are not. So what is an i Goffal? A few years back, a group of goffal programming wizards, mind hackers, philosophers, got together to coin the term i Goffal, and it is an upgrade for the mind, for our collective memory, a brotherhood, working together to show the world who we are. Have a nice day my brothers and sisters. We currently have a very interesting debate on going here http://www.facebook.com/?tid=1811425495164&sk=messages#!/topic.php?uid=30984049647&topic=14832 but you can also join other discusions. If you wish to participate in an anonymous discussion or read more about the development of the iGoffal mindset you can visit and register(using an alias) with this forum http://goffalraps.informe.com/portal.html

513759366@facebook.com, 22916051461@facebook.com, 1607440588@facebook.com
